nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mord">∣</span><span class="mord">∣</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.17688em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
将缩放后的结果带入（1）式，我们发现分子分母同时缩放了<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mn>1</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mi>q</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">1/q</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mord">/</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">q</span></span></span></span></span>，因此相互抵消，所以缩放操作对所有数据点的几何距离都没有产生影响。<br>
结论：这个粗暴操作粗中有细，是可行的。<br>
-------- 注<br>
ESL书中的式4.45和4.46表示形式与本文（3）式（即PRML与MLAPP的形式）的起始形式不同，但可以统一起来：<br>
我们用（2）式表示最近点的距离<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>r</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><msup><mi>n</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">r^{(n^*)}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.89734em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">r</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.89734em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.763343em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.931em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> ，交换等号两边、两边同乘以分母得到：<br>

带入上式可得：<br>
<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>min</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mi>n</mi></msub><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>(</mo><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><msup><mrow></mrow><mi>T</mi></msup><mo>⋅</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>+</mo><mi>b</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><msup><mi>r</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><msup><mi>n</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><mo>=</mo><msup><mi>r</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><msup><mi>n</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mfrac><mn>1</mn><msup><mi>r</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><msup><mi>n</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\min_{n} y^{(n)}(\mathbf{w}{^T}\cdot\mathbf{x}^{(n)} + b) = r^{(n^*)} ||\mathbf{w}|| = r^{(n^*)} \frac{1}{r^{(n^*)}} = 1</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.138em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">∣</span><span class="mord">∣</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf" style="margin-right: 0.01597em;">w</span></span><span class="mord">∣</span><span class="mord">∣</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.2874em; vertical-align: -0.390065em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">r</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.89734em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.763343em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.931em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.845108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.60994em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">r</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.828664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.82866em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.54234em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.75928em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.794em; margin-right: 0.1em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.394em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.390065em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span></span><br>
取最左和最右两项联立相等便回到了我们的（4）式上。</li>
</ul>
</blockquote>
<h5 id="trick-2">Trick 2</h5>
<p>当然，约束（4）本身是一个对数据集合批处理的运算，这样一个运算作为约束条件也不太好操作，嗯，我是说，我们的拉格朗日乘子可是一对一地处理约束条件的。于是我们把这个batch操作个例化，（4）式被转述为以下约束条件的集合：</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mtable side="right"><mlabeledtr><mtd><mtext>(6)</mtext></mtd><mtd><mrow><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>(</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mi>T</mi></msup><mo>⋅</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>+</mo><mi>b</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>≥</mo><mn>1</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow></mtd></mlabeledtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">y^{(n)} (\mathbf{w}^{T}\cdot\mathbf{x}^{(n)} + b) \geq 1, n = 1,...,N \tag{6}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.188em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf" style="margin-right: 0.01597em;">w</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.891331em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">T</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋅</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.02133em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf">x</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathit">b</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≥</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.87777em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">N</span></span><span class="tag"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.188em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">6</span></span><span class="mord">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>这里当且仅当<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>(</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo separator="true">,</mo><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(\mathbf{x}^{(n)}, y^{(n)})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.138em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf">x</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span> 为到决策边界最近的点时取到等号，其余点的情况均严格大于1。由于决策边界在我们问题的情形下是必定存在的，所以等号是必定能够取到的，我们因此可以确定（4）和（6）式说的是同一件事情。</p>
<h5 id="trick-3">Trick 3</h5>
<p>最后一个小Trick的动机是方便计算，我们把（5）式的二阶范数开平方（方便求导）、求倒数后从最大化转换为形如（7）式的最小化目标的形式。我们再把（6）式略变形后作为（8）式描述约束条件，这样便构成了改造后的不等式约束优化问题。<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mtable side="right"><mlabeledtr><mtd><mtext>(7)</mtext></mtd><mtd><mrow><munder><mi>min</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>b</mi></mrow></munder><msup><mfrac><mrow><mo fence="true">∣</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><mo fence="true">∣</mo></mrow><mn>2</mn></mfrac><mn>2</mn></msup></mrow></mtd></mlabeledtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\min_{\mathbf{w}, b} \frac{\left||\mathbf{w}|\right|}{2}^{2} \tag{7}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.51922em; vertical-align: -0.888216em;"></span><span class="mop op-limits"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.66786em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.04789em; margin-left: 0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathbf mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01597em;">w</span></span><span class="mpunct mtight">,</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">b</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -2.7em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class=""><span class="mop">min</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888216em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.427em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.314em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">2</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.677em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">∣</span><span class="mord">∣</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf" style="margin-right: 0.01597em;">w</span></span><span class="mord">∣</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">∣</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.686em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.63101em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.8799em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="tag"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.51922em; vertical-align: -0.888216em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">7</span></span><span class="mord">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mtable side="right"><mlabeledtr><mtd><mtext>(8)</mtext></mtd><mtd><mrow><mtext>s.t.&nbsp;</mtext><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>(</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mi>T</mi></msup><mo>⋅</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>+</mo><mi>b</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>≤</mo><mn>0</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow></mtd></mlabeledtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text{s.t.  } 1 - y^{(n)} (\mathbf{w}^{T}\cdot\mathbf{x}^{(n)} + b) \leq 0, n=1,...,N \tag{8}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.72777em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">s.t.&nbsp;</span></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.188em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf" style="margin-right: 0.01597em;">w</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.891331em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">T</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋅</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.02133em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf">x</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathit">b</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≤</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.87777em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">N</span></span><span class="tag"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.188em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">8</span></span><span class="mord">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>瞥一眼原来的（3）式，改造后的问题已经是一个规整的带不等式约束的二次优化问题了。</p>
<h4 id="构建拉格朗日函数求解优化问题">1.4 构建拉格朗日函数求解优化问题</h4>
<p>于是我们可以愉快地引入拉格朗日乘子来构造无约束优化问题：</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mtable><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mi>L</mi><mo>(</mo><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>b</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>α</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><munder><mi>min</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>b</mi></mrow></munder><mo fence="false">{</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mn>2</mn></mfrac><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mi>T</mi></msup><mo>⋅</mo><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mo>+</mo><munder><mi>max</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mi mathvariant="bold-italic">α</mi></munder><mo fence="false">{</mo><munderover><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>N</mi></munderover><msup><mi>α</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo fence="false">[</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>(</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mi>T</mi></msup><mo>⋅</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>+</mo><mi>b</mi><mo>)</mo><mo fence="false">]</mo><mo fence="false">}</mo><mo fence="false">}</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><munder><mi>min</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>b</mi></mrow></munder><mo fence="false">{</mo><munder><mi>max</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mi mathvariant="bold-italic">α</mi></munder><mo fence="false">{</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mn>2</mn></mfrac><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mi>T</mi></msup><mo>⋅</mo><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mo>+</mo><munderover><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>N</mi></munderover><msup><mi>α</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo L(\mathbf{w}, b, \mathbf{\alpha}) &amp;amp;= \min_{\mathbf{w}, b}\bigg\{\frac{1}{2}\mathbf{w}^{T}\cdot \mathbf{w} + \max_{\bm{\alpha}}\big\{\sum_{n=1}^{N}\alpha^{(n)}\big[1-y^{(n)}(\mathbf{w}^{T} \cdot \mathbf{x}^{(n)} + b)\big]\big\}\bigg\} \\ &amp;amp;= \min_{\mathbf{w}, b}\bigg\{\max_{\bm{\alpha}}\big\{\frac{1}{2}\mathbf{w}^{T}\cdot \mathbf{w} + vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.25em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.25em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.82834em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">(9)</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 3.14545em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>其中，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="bold-italic">α</mi><mo>=</mo><mo>(</mo><msup><mi>α</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><msup><mi>α</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>N</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>)</mo><mo>≥</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\bm{\alpha} = (\alpha^{(1)},...,\alpha^{(N)}) \geq 0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.44444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord boldsymbol">α</span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.138em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">N</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≥</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span> 的每一项是每个数据点对应约束条件的拉格朗日乘子，第一个min为我们原始的优化目标，后一个max则迫使最优解满足（8）中的约束条件。</p>
<p>三个变量的优化做起来很复杂，我们于是希望通过利用拉格朗日函数的对偶性，交换max（固定拉格朗日乘子求偏导数以试图获得w和b的表示）和min的求解顺序，把问题转化成由单一的拉格朗日乘子表示的形式（转化后的问题能确保最优解与原问题一致吗？）。</p>
<p>为了得到由式（7）、（8）所描述问题的对偶形式，令<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mtable side="right"><mlabeledtr><mtd><mtext>(10)</mtext></mtd><mtd><mrow><mfrac><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">∂</mi><mi>L</mi><mo>(</mo><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>b</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">∂</mi><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi></mrow></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mo>−</mo><munderover><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>N</mi></munderover><msup><mi>α</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>=</mo><mn mathvariant="bold">0</mn></mrow></mtd></mlabeledtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\frac {\partial L(\mathbf{w}, b)}{\partial\mathbf{w}} = \mathbf{w} - \sum_{n=1}^{N}\alpha^{(n)} y^{(n)}\mathbf{x}^{(n)} = \mathbf{0} \tag{10}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.113em; vertical-align: -0.686em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.427em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.314em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord" style="margin-right: 0.05556em;">∂</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf" style="margin-right: 0.01597em;">w</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.677em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord" style="margin-right: 0.05556em;">∂</span><span class="mord mathit">L</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf" style="margin-right: 0.01597em;">w</span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathit">b</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.686em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.66666em; vertical-align: -1.26711em;"></span><span class="mop op-limits"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.82834em;"><span class="" style="top: -1.88289em; 得到<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mtable side="right"><mlabeledtr><mtd><mtext>(11)</mtext></mtd><mtd><mrow><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mo>=</mo><munderover><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>N</mi></munderover><msup><mi>α</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup></mrow></mtd></mlabeledtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathbf{w} = \sum_{n=1}^{N} \alpha^{(n)} y^{(n)} \mathbf{x}^{(n)} \tag{11}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.44444em; <p>再令<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mtable side="right"><mlabeledtr><mtd><mtext>(12)</mtext></mtd><mtd><mrow><mfrac><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">∂</mi><mi>L</mi><mo>(</mo><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>b</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">∂</mi><mi>b</mi></mrow></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><msup><mi>α</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>→</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>=</mo><msup><mi>α</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup></mrow></mtd></mlabeledtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\frac{\partial L(\mathbf{w}, b)}{\partial b} = -\alpha^{(n)} y^{(n)} = 0 \rightarrow 0 = \alpha^{(n)} y^{(n)} \tag{12}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.113em; <p>把（11）、（12）代回（9）式并分别化解各项，<br>

scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mtext>(14)</mtext></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\begin{aligned} \frac{1}{2}\mathbf{w}^{T} \cdot \mathbf{w} &amp;amp;= \frac{1}{2}(\sum_{n=1}^{N} \alpha^{(n)} y^{(n)}\mathbf{x}^{(n)})^T \cdot (\sum_{m=1}^{N} \alpha^{(m)} y^{(m)}\mathbf{x}^{(m)}) \\ &amp;amp;= \frac{1}{2}\sum_{n=1}^{N} \sum_{m=1}^{N} \alpha^{(n)} \alpha^{(m)} y^{(n)} y^{(m)} {\mathbf{x}^{(n)}}^T \mathbf{x}^{(m)}  &amp;amp; \text{(13)}\\ \sum_{n=1}^{N}\alpha^{(n)}\big[1-y^{(n)}(\mathbf{w}^{T} \cdot \mathbf{x}^{(n)} + b)\big] &amp;amp;= \sum_{n=1}^{N}\alpha^{(n)} - \sum_{n=1}^{N}\alpha^{(n)}y^{(n)}\mathbf{w}^{T} \cdot \mathbf{x}^{n} - b \sum_{n=1}^{N}\alpha^{(n)}y^{(n)} \\ &amp;amp;= \sum_{n=1}^{N}\alpha^{(n)} - \sum_{n=1}^{N}\alpha^{(n)}y^{(n)}\mathbf{w}^{T} \cdot \mathbf{x}^{n} &amp;amp; \text{(带入(10)式消元)} \\ &amp;amp;= \sum_{n=1}^{N}\alpha^{(n)} - \sum_{n=1}^{N}\alpha^{(n)}y^{(n)}\big[\sum_{m=1}^{N}\alpha^{(m)}y^{(m)}{\mathbf{x}^{(m)}}^{T} \cdot \mathbf{x}^{n}\big] \\ &amp;amp;= \sum_{n=1}^{N}\alpha^{(n)} - \sum_{n=1}^{N}\sum_{m=1}^{N}\alpha^{(n)}\alpha^{(m)}y^{(n)}y^{(m)}{\mathbf{x}^{(m)}}^{T} \cdot \mathbf{x}^{n} &amp;amp;\text{(14)} \end{aligned}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span <p>将式(13)加上（14）最终得到原问题的对偶形式：<br>

{\mathbf{x}^{(n)}}^{T} \cdot \mathbf{x}^{(m)} \bigg\} \tag{15} \\ \text{s.t. } \alpha^{(n)} \geq 0, n = 1,...,N \\ \sum_{n=1}^{N}\alpha^{(n)} y^{(n)} = 0 </annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="mord">5</span></span><span class="mord">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>有了这个目标函数，就可以用<a href="https://zh.wikipedia.org/wiki/%E5%BA%8F%E5%88%97%E6%9C%80%E5%B0%8F%E4%BC%98%E5%8C%96%E7%AE%97%E6%B3%95">序列最小优化算法</a>求得最优解：<br>
<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi mathvariant="bold-italic">α</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>=</mo><mo>[</mo><msup><msup><mi>α</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><msup><msup><mi>α</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>N</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\bm{\alpha}^{*} = [{\alpha^*}^{(1)},...,{\alpha^*}^{(N)}]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.688696em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord boldsymbol">α</span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.2166em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.966596em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.1416em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.966596em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.1416em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">N</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<blockquote>
<p>那么这个最优解是否是（9）式所描述问题的最优解呢？答案是肯定的，因为<br>
1.我们的优化问题是凸优化问题；<br>
2我们的优化问题满足KKT条件：<br>
取得<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>α</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathbf{\alpha}^{*}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.688696em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>时，我们有：<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo fence="true">{</mo><mtable><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mi>T</mi></msup><mo>⋅</mo><msup><mi 前面三个条件是我们直接处理过的式子，最后一个条件为什么满足了呢？ 结合（9）式，我们看到，这个条件的第二项（右项）是被最大化的项，</p>
<ul>
<li>当<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>(</mo><msup><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mi>T</mi></msup><mo>⋅</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>+</mo><msup><mi>b</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>)</mo><mo>&amp;lt;</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">1 - y^{(n)} (\mathbf{w^{*}}^T \cdot \mathbf{x}^{(n)} + b^* ) &amp;lt; <li>当<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>(</mo><msup><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mi>T</mi></msup><mo>⋅</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>+</mo><msup><mi>b</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">1 - y^{(n)} (\mathbf{w^{*}}^T \cdot \mathbf{x}^{(n)} + b^* ) = 0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.72777em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">b</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>时，数据点是离决策边界最近的点，此时<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><msup><mi>α</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>&amp;gt;</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\alpha^*}^{(n)} &amp;gt; 0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.0057em; vertical-align: -0.0391em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.966596em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.1416em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">&gt;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span> (否则拉格朗日乘子全部为0)，乘积仍然是零。</li>
</ul>
<p>所以我们的第四个条件对于每一个数据点都成立。 正因为在这个问题上，KKT的所有条件都满足，所以，我们通过对偶问题求得的最优解，也即是原问题的最优解。</p>
</blockquote>
<p>把最优解代回（11）并利用最近点使得决策方程值为1的条件求解参数，得到：<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mtable><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><munderover><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>N</mi></munderover><msup><msup><mi>α</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><msup><mi>b</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><msup><mi>n</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>−</mo><msup><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mi>T</mi></msup><mo>⋅</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><msup><mi>n</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{aligned} \mathbf{w}^{*} &amp;amp;= \sum_{n=1}^{N} {\alpha^*}^{(n)} y^{(n)} \mathbf{x}^{(n)} \\ b^{*} &amp;amp;= y^{(n^{*})} - \mathbf{w^*}^{T} \cdot {\mathbf{x}^{(n^{*})}} \end{aligned}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 5.02538em; vertical-align: -2.26269em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mtable"><span class="col-align-r"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.76269em;"><span class="" style="top: -4.76269em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.82834em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf" style="margin-right: 0.01597em;">w</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.738696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -2.22565em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.82834em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">b</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.738696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.26269em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="col-align-l"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.76269em;"><span class="" style="top: -4.76269em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.82834em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mop op-limits"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.82834em;"><span class="" style="top: -1.88289em; margin-left: 0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.05em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mrel mtight">=</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.05001em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.05em;"></span><span class=""><span class="mop op-symbol large-op">∑</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -4.30001em; margin-left: 0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.05em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">N</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.26711em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.738696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.0166em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.1916em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf">x</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -2.22565em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.82834em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.94734em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.763343em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.931em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf" style="margin-right: 0.01597em;">w</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.738696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.969927em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.1916em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">T</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋅</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf">x</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.94734em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.763343em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.931em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.26269em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>其中 <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>(</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><msup><mi>n</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo separator="true">,</mo><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><msup><mi>n</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(\mathbf{x}^{(n^{*})}, y^{(n^{*})})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.14734em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf">x</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.89734em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.763343em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.931em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.89734em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.763343em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.931em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span>为距离决策边界最近的数据点，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><msup><mi>n</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathbf{x}^{(n^{*})}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.89734em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf">x</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.89734em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.763343em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.931em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>就是我们梦寐以求的支持向量了</p>
<blockquote>
<p>注：<br>
这里求<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>b</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b^*</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">b</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>的做法和ESL中的相同，找任意一个支持向量数据点计算得到。PRML书中建议我们计算所有支持向量取平均以曾强鲁棒，</p>
</blockquote>
<h4 id="预测">1.5 预测</h4>
<p>利用最优参数得到预测函数：<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mtable side="right"><mlabeledtr><mtd><mtext>(16)</mtext></mtd><mtd><mtable><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mi>y</mi><mo>(</mo><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><msup><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mi>T</mi></msup><mo>⋅</mo><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mo>+</mo><msup><mi>b</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><munderover><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>N</mi></munderover><msup><msup><mi>α</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><msup><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mi>T</mi></msup><mo>⋅</mo><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mo>+</mo><msup><mi>b</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable></mtd></mlabeledtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{aligned} y(\mathbf{x}) &amp;amp;= {\mathbf{w}^*}^{T} \cdot \mathbf{x} + b^* \\ &amp;amp;= \sum_{n=1}^{N} \mathbf{\alpha^*}^{(n)} y^{(n)} {\mathbf{x}^{(n)}}^{T} \cdot \mathbf{x} + b^* \end{aligned} \tag{16}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 5.02538em; vertical-align: -2.26269em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mtable"><span class="col-align-r"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.76269em;"><span class="" style="top: -5.6211em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.82834em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf">x</span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.13276em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.82834em;"></span><span class="mord"></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.26269em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="col-align-l"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.76269em;"><span class="" style="top: -5.6211em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.82834em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf" style="margin-right: 0.01597em;">w</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.738696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf">x</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.16923em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.3909em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">T</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋅</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf">x</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">b</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.738696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.26269em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="tag"><span class="strut" style="height: 5.02538em; vertical-align: -2.26269em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mord">6</span></span><span class="mord">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
在这个求和计算中非支持向量的拉格朗日乘子都为0，所以实际上我们只需要保存训练集合中的少部分支持向量及对应的拉格朗日参数<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><msup><mi>α</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><msup><mi>n</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\alpha^*}^{(n^*)}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.975936em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.975936em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.1416em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.763343em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.931em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 即可。</p>
<p>从决策函数上看，给定输入，这个模型对输入特征进行线性组合，加上偏置项后输出预测。</p>
<p>如果牵涉到特征映射，我们可以把上式写成下面的形式：<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mtable side="right"><mlabeledtr><mtd><mtext>(17)</mtext></mtd><mtd><mtable><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mi>y</mi><mo>(</mo><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><msup><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mi>T</mi></msup><mo>⋅</mo><mi>ϕ</mi><mo>(</mo><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>+</mo><msup><mi>b</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><munderover><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>N</mi></munderover><msup><msup><mi>α</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mi>ϕ</mi><mo>(</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><msup><mo>)</mo><mi>T</mi></msup><mo>⋅</mo><mi>ϕ</mi><mo>(</mo><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>+</mo><msup><mi>b</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable></mtd></mlabeledtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{aligned} y(\mathbf{x}) &amp;amp;= {\mathbf{w}^*}^{T} \cdot \phi(\mathbf{x}) + b^* \\ &amp;amp;= \sum_{n=1}^{N} \mathbf{\alpha^*}^{(n)} y^{(n)} \phi({\mathbf{x}^{(n)}})^{T} \cdot \phi(\mathbf{x}) + b^* \end{aligned} \tag{17}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 5.02538em; vertical-align: -2.26269em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mtable"><span class="col-align-r"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.76269em;"><span class="" style="top: -5.6211em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.82834em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf">x</span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.13276em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.82834em;"></span><span class="mord"></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.26269em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="col-align-l"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.76269em;"><span class="" style="top: -5.6211em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.82834em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf" style="margin-right: 0.01597em;">w</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.738696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.969927em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.1916em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose"><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.891331em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em;
