encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{cases} \frac{\partial L}{\partial \mathbf{w^*}} = \mathbf{0}, \frac{\partial L}{\partial b^*} = 0, \frac{\partial L}{\partial \mathbf{\alpha^*}} = \mathbf{0}, \frac{\partial L}{\partial \mathbf{\xi^*}} = \mathbf{0},  \frac{\partial L}{\partial \mathbf{\mu^*}} =\mathbf{0}  \\ {\alpha^*}^{(n)} \geq 0, n = 1, ..., N\\ 
1 - {\xi^*}^{(n)} - y^{(n)} (\mathbf{w^{*}}^T \cdot \mathbf{x}^{(n)} + b^* ) \leq 0, n = 1, ..., N\\ {\alpha^*}^{(n)}(1 - {\xi^*}^{(n)}- y^{(n)} (\mathbf{w^{*}}^T \cdot \mathbf{x}^{(n)} + b^* )) = 0, n = 1, ..., N\\ 
{\mu^*}^{(n)} \geq0,n=1,...,N \\
-{\xi^*}^{(n)}\leq0 \\
{\mu^*}^{(n)}{\xi^*}^{(n)} = 0
\end{cases}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 10.2em; vertical-align: -4.85002em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">μ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.966596em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.1416em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.04601em;">ξ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.97234em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.14734em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 4.81455em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
注意，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>α</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\alpha^{(n)}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.888em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>的最优解可以通过线性变换转换为<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>ξ</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\xi^{(n)}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.08244em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.04601em;">ξ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>的最优解；当<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>−</mo><msup><msup><mi>ξ</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>&amp;lt;</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">-{\xi^*}^{(n)}&amp;lt;0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.16678em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord">−</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.04601em;">ξ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.97234em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.14734em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">&lt;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>时，必须有<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><msup><mi>μ</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\mu^*}^{(n)}=0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.16104em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">μ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.966596em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.1416em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>才能使得目标函数最大化。综上，KKT所有条件均得到满足，所以对偶问题的最优解也是原问题的最优解。</p>
<h5 id="预测-1">1.6.4 预测</h5>
<p>预测函数同式（16）或（18）（kernel trick的话）。所有<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><msup><mi>α</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>&amp;gt;</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\alpha^*}^{(n)}&amp;gt;0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.0057em; vertical-align: -0.0391em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.966596em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.1416em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">&gt;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span> 的数据点成为支持向量，它们满足<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>(</mo><msup><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mi>T</mi></msup><mo>⋅</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>+</mo><msup><mi>b</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><msup><msup><mi>ξ</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">y^{(n)}({\mathbf{w}^*}^T \cdot \mathbf{x}^{(n)} + b^*) =1-{\xi^*}^{(n)}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.16993em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf" style="margin-right: 0.01597em;">w</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.919927em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.1416em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">T</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋅</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.97133em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf">x</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">b</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.72777em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.16678em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.04601em;">ξ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.97234em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.14734em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>。<br>
根据式子(25)，当<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><msup><mi>α</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>&amp;lt;</mo><mi>C</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\alpha^*}^{(n)}&amp;lt;C</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.0057em; vertical-align: -0.0391em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.966596em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.1416em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">&lt;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">C</span></span></span></span></span>时，我们有<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><msup><mi>μ</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>&amp;gt;</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\mu^*}^{(n)}&amp;gt;0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.16104em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">μ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.966596em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.1416em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">&gt;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>，因此必然有<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><msup><mi>ξ</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\xi^*}^{(n)}=0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.16678em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.04601em;">ξ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.97234em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.14734em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>说明这些支持向量在间隔边缘（即他们是原来硬间隔下的支持向量）。而当<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><msup><mi>α</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>=</mo><mi>C</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\alpha^*}^{(n)}=C</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.966596em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.966596em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.1416em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">C</span></span></span></span></span>时，有<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><msup><mi>μ</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\mu^*}^{(n)}=0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.16104em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">μ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.966596em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.1416em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>，意味着<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><msup><mi>ξ</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>&amp;gt;</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\xi^*}^{(n)}&amp;gt;0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.16678em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.04601em;">ξ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.97234em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.14734em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">&gt;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>。这部分支持向量为错分类点（<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><msup><mi>ξ</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>&amp;gt;</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\xi^*}^{(n)}&amp;gt;1</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.16678em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.04601em;">ξ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.97234em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.14734em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">&gt;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span></span>），或者是间隔内部的点（<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mn>0</mn><mo>&amp;lt;</mo><msup><msup><mi>ξ</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>≤</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">0&amp;lt;{\xi^*}^{(n)}\leq1</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68354em; vertical-align: -0.0391em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">&lt;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.16678em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.04601em;">ξ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.97234em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.14734em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span></span>）。<br>
参数<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathbf{w^*}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.688696em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf" style="margin-right: 0.01597em;">w</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>的计算公式与硬间隔条件下的相同，做出贡献的是所有类别的支持向量：<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>=</mo><munderover><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>N</mi></munderover><msup><msup><mi>α</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathbf{w}^{*} = \sum_{n=1}^{N} {\alpha^*}^{(n)} y^{(n)} \mathbf{x}^{(n)}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.738696em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf" style="margin-right: 0.01597em;">w</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.738696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 3.09545em; vertical-align: -1.26711em;"></span><span class="mop op-limits"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.82834em;"><span class="" style="top: -1.88289em; margin-left: 0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.05em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mrel mtight">=</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.05001em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.05em;"></span><span class=""><span class="mop op-symbol large-op">∑</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -4.30001em; margin-left: 0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.05em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">N</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.26711em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.738696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.0166em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.1916em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf">x</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
对于参数<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>b</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b^*</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">b</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>的计算，我们可以利用任意一个硬间隔边界上的支持向量<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>(</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><msup><mi>n</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo separator="true">,</mo><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><msup><mi>n</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(\mathbf{x}^{(n^*)}, y^{(n^*)})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.14734em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf">x</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.89734em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.763343em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.931em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.89734em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.763343em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.931em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span>得到：<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mtable><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><msup><mi>b</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><msup><mi>n</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>−</mo><msup><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mi>T</mi></msup><mo>⋅</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><msup><mi>n</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><msup><mi>n</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>−</mo><munderover><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>N</mi></munderover><msup><msup><mi>α</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><msup><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mi>T</mi></msup><mo>⋅</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><msup><mi>n</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><msup><mi>n</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>−</mo><munderover><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>N</mi></munderover><msup><msup><mi>α</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mi>k</mi><mo>(</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo separator="true">,</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><msup><mi>n</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\begin{aligned}
 b^{*} &amp;amp;= y^{(n^{*})} - \mathbf{w^*}^{T} \cdot {\mathbf{x}^{(n^{*})}} \\&amp;amp;=y^{(n^*)}-\sum_{n=1}^N{\alpha^*}^{(n)}y^{(n)} {\mathbf{x}^{(n)}}^T 
 \cdot \mathbf{x}^{(n^*)} \\
 &amp;amp;=y^{(n^*)}-\sum_{n=1}^N{\alpha^*}^{(n)}y^{(n)} k(\mathbf{x}^{(n)}, \mathbf{x}^{(n^*)})
 \end{aligned}
 </annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 8.42083em; vertical-align: -3.96041em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mtable"><span class="col-align-r"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 4.46041em;"><span class="" style="top: -7.31882em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.82834em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">b</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.738696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -4.83049em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.82834em;"></span><span class="mord"></span></span><span class="" style="top: -1.43504em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.82834em;"></span><span class="mord"></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 3.96041em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="col-align-l"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 4.46041em;"><span class="" style="top: -7.31882em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.82834em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.94734em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 3.96041em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
注意最后这里写成了kernel的形式。同样的，按照PRML的建议，可以对支持向量求平均以增强鲁棒，只是这个平均是对所有<strong>在硬间隔边界上的支持向量</strong>进行操作。</p>
<h3 id="损失函数的视角">2. 损失函数的视角</h3>
<h4 id="分类">2.1 分类</h4>
<p>相对几何视角，损失函数设计的动机让我这种缺乏背景的民科比较难以猜测，也许只能硬这么理解。引入铰链损失(Hinge Loss)：<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mtable side="right"><mlabeledtr><mtd><mtext>(28)</mtext></mtd><mtd><mtable><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><msub><mi>L</mi><mrow><mi>h</mi><mi>i</mi><mi>n</mi><mi>g</mi><mi>e</mi></mrow></msub></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>max</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mo>(</mo><mn>0</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><mi>ξ</mi><mo>−</mo><mi>y</mi><mo>⋅</mo><mo>(</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mi>T</mi></msup><mo>⋅</mo><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>b</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mo>[</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><mi>ξ</mi><mo>−</mo><mi>y</mi><mo>⋅</mo><mo>(</mo><mrow><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mi mathvariant="bold">T</mi></msup><mo>⋅</mo><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="bold">b</mi></mrow><mo>)</mo><msub><mo>]</mo><mo>+</mo></msub></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable></mtd></mlabeledtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\begin{aligned}
L_{hinge} &amp;amp;= \max(0, 1-\xi - y\cdot(\mathbf{w}^T \cdot \mathbf{x} + b)) \\&amp;amp;= [1- \xi - y\cdot(\mathbf{w^T \cdot \mathbf{x} + b})]_+
\tag{28}
\end{aligned}

0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋅</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf"
