vertical-align: -0.283108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.04601em;">ξ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.41689em; margin-left: -0.04601em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.283108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.97234em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.14734em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>，也就是说预测值存在两种可能的情况：1）当疏松变量<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><msubsup><mi>ξ</mi><mi>l</mi><mo>∗</mo></msubsup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\xi_l^*}^{(n)} =0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.25545em; vertical-align: -0.283108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.04601em;">ξ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.41689em; margin-left: -0.04601em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.283108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.97234em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.14734em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>时，预测值正好落在<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>−</mo><mi>ϵ</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">-\epsilon</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.66666em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord">−</span><span class="mord mathit">ϵ</span></span></span></span></span>边界上，即<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mover accent="true"><mi>y</mi><mo>^</mo></mover><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>=</mo><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>−</mo><mi>ϵ</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\hat{y}^{(n)}=y^{(n)} - \epsilon</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.08244em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord accent"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.69444em;"><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="accent-body" style="left: -0.19444em;">^</span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.19444em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.08244em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathit">ϵ</span></span></span></span></span>；2）当<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><msubsup><mi>ξ</mi><mi>l</mi><mo>∗</mo></msubsup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>&amp;gt;</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\xi_l^*}^{(n)}&amp;gt;0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.25545em; vertical-align: -0.283108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.04601em;">ξ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.41689em; margin-left: -0.04601em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.283108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.97234em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.14734em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">&gt;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>时，预测值在<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>−</mo><mi>ϵ</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">-\epsilon</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.66666em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord">−</span><span class="mord mathit">ϵ</span></span></span></span></span>阙值之下，受益于疏松变量拉低了下边界，该预测值才被视作预测正确。以同样的方式可以解读<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi>α</mi><mi>u</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo>&amp;gt;</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\alpha_{u}^{(n)} &amp;gt; 0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.16139em; vertical-align: -0.116592em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.0448em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.58341em; margin-left: -0.0037em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">u</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.2198em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.116592em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">&gt;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>对于上边界预测的影响。</p>
<p>再者，一个数据对应的<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi>α</mi><mi>u</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msubsup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\alpha_{u}^{(n)}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.16139em; vertical-align: -0.116592em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.0448em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.58341em; margin-left: -0.0037em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">u</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.2198em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.116592em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>和<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi>α</mi><mi>l</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msubsup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\alpha_{l}^{(n)}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.34611em; vertical-align: -0.301308em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.0448em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.39869em; margin-left: -0.0037em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.2198em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301308em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>不可能同时取非零值。对于一个预测值<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mover accent="true"><mi>y</mi><mo>^</mo></mover><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\hat{y}^{(n)}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.08244em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord accent"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.69444em;"><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="accent-body" style="left: -0.19444em;">^</span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.19444em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>，它或者大于、或者小于目标值<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">y^{(n)}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.08244em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>，因此其对应的<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi>α</mi><mi>u</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo separator="true">,</mo><msubsup><mi>α</mi><mi>l</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msubsup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\alpha_{u}^{(n)},\alpha_{l}^{(n)}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.34611em; vertical-align: -0.301308em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.0448em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.58341em; margin-left: -0.0037em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">u</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.2198em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.116592em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.0448em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.39869em; margin-left: -0.0037em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.2198em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301308em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>中至多有一个可以为非零，因为非零意味着该预测值在上下硬边界上或者硬边界之外，而因为<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>ϵ</mi><mo>&amp;gt;</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\epsilon&amp;gt;0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.5782em; vertical-align: -0.0391em;"></span><span class="mord mathit">ϵ</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">&gt;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>，上下边界间距为<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mn>2</mn><mi>ϵ</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">2\epsilon</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mord mathit">ϵ</span></span></span></span></span>，这样一来，一个预测值不可能既在<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>−</mo><mi>ϵ</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">y^{(n)}-\epsilon</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.08244em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathit">ϵ</span></span></span></span></span>的下边界上，又在<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>+</mo><mi>ϵ</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">y^{(n)} + \epsilon</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.08244em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathit">ϵ</span></span></span></span></span>的上边界上（或者比上边界还要高的位置）。</p>
<p>对于第四个KKT条件，位于<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>ϵ</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\epsilon</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathit">ϵ</span></span></span></span></span>边界上的数据点有<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><msubsup><mi>ξ</mi><mi>u</mi><mo>∗</mo></msubsup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\xi_{u}^*}^{(n)}=0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.21934em; vertical-align: -0.247em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.04601em;">ξ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.453em; margin-left: -0.04601em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">u</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.247em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.97234em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.14734em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>或者<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><msubsup><mi>ξ</mi><mi>l</mi><mo>∗</mo></msubsup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\xi_{l}^*}^{(n)}=0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.25545em; vertical-align: -0.283108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.04601em;">ξ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.41689em; margin-left: -0.04601em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.283108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.97234em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.14734em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>，条件满足；而当<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>−</mo><msup><msubsup><mi>ξ</mi><mi>u</mi><mo>∗</mo></msubsup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>&amp;lt;</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">-{\xi_{u}^*}^{(n)}&amp;lt;0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.21934em; vertical-align: -0.247em;"></span><span class="mord">−</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.04601em;">ξ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.453em; margin-left: -0.04601em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">u</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.247em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.97234em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.14734em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">&lt;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>或者<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>−</mo><msup><msubsup><mi>ξ</mi><mi>l</mi><mo>∗</mo></msubsup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>&amp;lt;</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">-{\xi_{l}^*}^{(n)}&amp;lt;0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.25545em; vertical-align: -0.283108em;"></span><span class="mord">−</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.04601em;">ξ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.41689em; margin-left: -0.04601em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.283108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.97234em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.14734em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">&lt;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><msubsup><mi>μ</mi><mi>l</mi><mo>∗</mo></msubsup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo separator="true">,</mo><msup><msubsup><mi>μ</mi><mi>u</mi><mo>∗</mo></msubsup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\mu_l^*}^{(n)}, {\mu_u^*}^{(n)}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.2497em; vertical-align: -0.283108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">μ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.41689em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.283108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.966596em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.1416em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">μ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.453em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">u</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.247em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.966596em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.1416em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>只有取0值才能使得整个式子取得最大值，这个时候，条件式子仍然等于零，因此条件满足。</p>
<p>所以，KKT的所有条件均满足，对偶问题的最优解也是原问题的最优解。</p>
<p>由式（33）可知所有这些<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi>α</mi><mrow><mi>u</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>l</mi></mrow><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msubsup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\alpha_{u,l}^{(n)}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.48222em; vertical-align: -0.437416em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.0448em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.39869em; margin-left: -0.0037em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">u</span><span class="mpunct mtight">,</span><span class="mord mathit mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.2198em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.437416em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>非零的数据点会成为“支持向量”，为函数拟合贡献力量。这些数据点对应的函数预测值要么位于上下<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>ϵ</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\epsilon</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathit">ϵ</span></span></span></span></span>-边界上，要么在这个边界区域之外。而所有<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><msubsup><mi>α</mi><mi>u</mi><mo>∗</mo></msubsup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>=</mo><msup><msubsup><mi>α</mi><mi>l</mi><mo>∗</mo></msubsup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\alpha_{u}^*}^{(n)} = {\alpha_{l}^*}^{(n)} = 0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.2136em; vertical-align: -0.247em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.453em; margin-left: -0.0037em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">u</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.247em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.966596em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.1416em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.2497em; vertical-align: -0.283108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.41689em; margin-left: -0.0037em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.283108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.966596em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.1416em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>的数据点的预测值则都在<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>ϵ</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\epsilon</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathit">ϵ</span></span></span></span></span>-区域之内可以被严格地正确预测。</p>
<h5 id="表示参数">表示参数</h5>
<p>我们可以将参数表示如下：<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mtable><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>=</mo><munderover><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>N</mi></munderover><mo>(</mo><msubsup><mi>α</mi><mi>u</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo>−</mo><msubsup><mi>α</mi><mi>l</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo>)</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mtext>(40)</mtext></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><msup><mi>b</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>=</mo><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><msup><mi>n</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>−</mo><mi>ϵ</mi><mo>−</mo><msup><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mi>T</mi></msup><mo>⋅</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><msup><mi>n</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mtext>(41)</mtext></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\begin{aligned}
\mathbf{w^*}=\sum_{n=1}^N(\alpha_{u}^{(n)} - \alpha_{l}^{(n)}) \mathbf{x}^{(n)}  &amp;amp;\text{(40)}\\
b^* = y^{(n^*)} - \epsilon - \mathbf{w^*}^T \cdot \mathbf{x}^{(n^*)} &amp;amp;\text{(41)}
\end{aligned}
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 5.02538em; vertical-align: -2.26269em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mtable"><span class="col-align-r"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.76269em;"><span class="" style="top: -4.76269em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.82834em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf" style="margin-right: 0.01597em;">w</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.738696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.26269em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="col-align-l"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.76269em;"><span class="" style="top: -4.76269em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.82834em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">(40)</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -2.22565em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.82834em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">(41)</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.26269em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
其中，类似分类情况，部分的数据点——支持向量——贡献决策函数的预测。对于参数<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>b</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b^*</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">b</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>我们可以任意取一个满足如下条件的支持向量（下标<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>{</mo><mi>u</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>l</mi><mo>}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\{u,l\}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathit">u</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span></span>表示或）<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mo fence="true">{</mo><mtable><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><msubsup><mi>α</mi><mrow><mo>{</mo><mi>u</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>l</mi><mo>}</mo></mrow><mo>∗</mo></msubsup><mo>&amp;gt;</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><msubsup><mi>μ</mi><mrow><mo>{</mo><mi>u</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>l</mi><mo>}</mo></mrow><mo>∗</mo></msubsup><mo>&amp;gt;</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable></mrow><mo>⇒</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">{</mo><mtable><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><msubsup><mi>α</mi><mrow><mo>{</mo><mi>u</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>l</mi><mo>}</mo></mrow><mo>∗</mo></msubsup><mo>&amp;gt;</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><msubsup><mi>α</mi><mrow><mo>{</mo><mi>u</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>l</mi><mo>}</mo></mrow><mo>∗</mo></msubsup><mo>&amp;lt;</mo><mi>C</mi><mtext>&nbsp;由式（35）或（36）</mtext></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{cases}
\alpha_{\{u,l\}}^* &amp;gt;0 \\
\mu_{\{u,l\}}^*&amp;gt;0
\end{cases} \Rightarrow 
\begin{cases}
\alpha_{\{u,l\}}^* &amp;gt;0 \\
\alpha_{\{u,l\}}^* &amp;lt; C \text{   由式（35）或（36）}
\end{cases}
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 3.01em; vertical-align: -1.255em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;"><span class="delimsizing size4">{</span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mtable"><span class="col-align-l"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.755em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.755em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.008em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.378em; 根据KKT条件第四条，此时必须有<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><msubsup><mi>ξ</mi><mrow><mo>{</mo><mi>u</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>l</mi><mo>}</mo></mrow><mo>∗</mo></msubsup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\xi_{\{u,l\}}^*}^{(n)}=0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.46934em; vertical-align: -0.497em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.04601em;">ξ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.378em; margin-left: -0.04601em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">{</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">u</span><span class="mpunct mtight">,</span><span class="mord mathit mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span><span class="mclose mtight">}</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.497em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.97234em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.14734em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>。因此，满足这些条件的支持向量，它们的预测值位于<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>ϵ</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\epsilon</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathit">ϵ</span></span></span></span></span>-区间的边界上。我们利用其中任意一个，将它带入KKT条件最后两条中适用的那一条便得到：<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">w</mi><mi>T</mi></msup><mo>⋅</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>+</mo><mi>b</mi><mo>−</mo><msup><mi>y</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>−</mo><mi>ϵ</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathbf{w}^T \cdot \mathbf{x}^{(n)} + b - y^{(n)} -  \epsilon=0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.841331em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf" style="margin-right: 0.01597em;">w</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.841331em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">T</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋅</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.97133em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf">x</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.77777em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord mathit">b</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.08244em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathit">ϵ</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>从而求得<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>b</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b^*</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">b</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
当然，根据PRML的建议，为所有满足条件的支持向量计算<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>b</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b^*</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">b</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>值并求平均会更robust。<br>
这样我们的最终的预测函数为：<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>y</mi><mo>(</mo><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><munderover><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>N</mi></munderover><mo>(</mo><msup><msubsup><mi>α</mi><mi>u</mi><mo>∗</mo></msubsup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>−</mo><msup><msubsup><mi>α</mi><mi>l</mi><mo>∗</mo></msubsup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>)</mo><msup><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mi>T</mi></msup><mo>⋅</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>+</mo><msup><mi>b</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
y(\mathbf{x}) = \sum_{n=1}^N({\alpha_u^*}^{(n)} - {\alpha_l^*}^{(n)}) {\mathbf{x}^{(n)}}^T \cdot \mathbf{x}^{(n)} + b^*
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf">x</span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 3.09545em; vertical-align: -1.26711em;"></span><span class="mop op-limits"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.82834em;"><span class="" style="top: -1.88289em; margin-left: 0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.05em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mrel mtight">=</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.05001em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.05em;"></span><span class=""><span class="mop op-symbol large-op">∑</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -4.30001em; margin-left: 0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.05em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">N</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.26711em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.738696em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.453em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.41923em; margin-left: -0.0037em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">b</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.738696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
可以写成kernel的形式：<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>y</mi><mo>(</mo><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><munderover><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>N</mi></munderover><mo>(</mo><msup><msubsup><mi>α</mi><mi>u</mi><mo>∗</mo></msubsup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>−</mo><msup><msubsup><mi>α</mi><mi>l</mi><mo>∗</mo></msubsup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>)</mo><mi>k</mi><mo>(</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo separator="true">,</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>)</mo><mo>+</mo><msup><mi>b</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
y(\mathbf{x}) = \sum_{n=1}^N({\alpha_u^*}^{(n)} - {\alpha_l^*}^{(n)}) k({\mathbf{x}^{(n)}}, \mathbf{x}^{(n)}) + b^*
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf">x</span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 3.09545em; vertical-align: -1.26711em;"></span><span class="mop op-limits"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.82834em;"><span class="" style="top: -1.88289em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.247em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.0166em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.1916em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.2666em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.247em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.0166em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.1916em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03148em;">k</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf">x</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf">x</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">n</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.738696em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">b</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.738696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<h2 id="算法分析">3. 算法分析</h2>
<ul>
<li>需要学习的参数个数：
<ol>
<li>带疏松变量的二类分类支持向量机对偶形式：<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>N</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">N</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">N</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li>带疏松变量的回归支持向量机对偶形式： <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mn>2</mn><mi>N</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">2N</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">N</span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>训练时间复杂度：
<ol>
<li>如果用通用的二次规划Solver，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>O</mi><mo>(</mo><msup><mi>n</mi><mn>3</mn></msup><mo>)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">O(n^3)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.06411em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">O</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.814108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">3</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li>如果用SMO算法，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>O</mi><mo>(</mo><msup><mi>n</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mo>)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">O(n^2)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.06411em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">O</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.814108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span>。PRML指出，在实践中根据具体任务的不同，平均时间开销与数据量的比例在<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>N</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">N</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">N</span></span></span></span></span>到<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>N</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">N^2</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.814108em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">N</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.814108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>之间。当使用线性核函数的时候，训练时间复杂度可以降低到O(N)</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>稳定性：<br>
算法对于异常值会很敏感，因为异常值有可能成为支持向量，干扰模型预测。</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="总结">总结</h2>
<p>呼，总算可以暂时告一个段落了。总的来说，SVM有许多trick，在图1.3中可以反映很多，在绘制这张图的时候，有很多之前粗粒度阅读所忽视的细节问题都被暴露出来，并且自己通过思考找到了答案，可谓收获很大。<br>
另外，之所以硬杠三个凸优化的对偶形式转换和KKT条件分析，是想熟练一下凸优化的操作套路，可谓经验收获很大。<br>
虽然SVM已经算不得最流行的机器学习算法，但是学习它仍然可以锻炼有价值的思考方式，特别是那种将直观的思想（最大化间隔）形式化求解的思考过程。这种技能说不定未来哪个时候一不当心就可以派上用场。<br>
SVM可谓线性模型的一个巅峰。抛去线性方程的形式，它就是一种稀疏化了的核方法，支持向量就是从稀疏操作中幸存下来的那些对预测最有用的训练数据点。<br>
最后，对比三本神书SVM的介绍，个人感觉PRML的阅读下来更顺畅一些。MLAPP则可以看作是对PRML的继承和补充。</p>
